\xd0\x96\xd0\xbe\xd2\x93\xd0\xb0\xd1\x80\xd1\x8b \xd1\x82\xd0\xb5\xd1\x85\xd0\xbd\xd0\xbe\xd0\xbb\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb3\xd0\xb8\xd1\x8f\xd2\x93\xd0\xb0 \xd0\xbd\xd0\xb5\xd0\xb3\xd1\x96\xd0\xb7\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb3\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbd \xd0\xbe\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb9 \xd0\xba\xd3\x99\xd1\x81\xd1\x96\xd0\xbf\xd0\xbe\xd1\x80\xd1\x8b\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb0\xd1\x80 \xd1\x81\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbd\xd1\x8b \xd2\x9b\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb7\xd1\x96\xd1\x80 63-\xd0\xba\xd0\xb5 \xd0\xb6\xd0\xb5\xd1\x82\xd0\xba\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbd. \xd0\x96\xd1\x8b\xd0\xbb \xd1\x81\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb9\xd1\x8b\xd0\xbd \xd0\xb1\xd2\xb1\xd0\xbb \xd0\xb5\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb5 158 \xd0\xbc\xd0\xbb\xd0\xbd \xd0\xbc\xc2\xb2 \xd0\xbc\xd0\xb0\xd2\x9b\xd1\x82\xd0\xb0-\xd0\xbc\xd0\xb0\xd1\x82\xd0\xb0 \xd0\xb1\xd2\xb1\xd0\xb9\xd1\x8b\xd0\xbc\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb0\xd1\x80\xd1\x8b \xd0\xbc\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbd 82 \xd0\xbc\xd1\x8b\xd2\xa3 \xd1\x82\xd0\xbe\xd0\xbd\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb0 \xd0\xb6\xd1\x96\xd0\xbf \xd0\xb8\xd1\x96\xd1\x80\xd1\x96\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb5\xd0\xb4\xd1\x96. \xd0\x9e\xd1\x81\xd1\x8b \xd3\xa9\xd0\xbd\xd1\x96\xd0\xbc\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb5\xd1\x80\xd1\x96\xd0\xbd \xd0\xa2\xd2\xaf\xd1\x80\xd1\x96\xd0\xba\xd0\xbc\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbd\xd1\x81\xd1\x82\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbd \xd3\x99\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbc\xd0\xbd\xd1\x96\xd2\xa3 \xd0\xb6\xd0\xbe\xd2\x93\xd0\xb0\xd1\x80\xd1\x8b \xd0\xb4\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbc\xd1\x8b\xd2\x93\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbd 30-\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbd \xd0\xb0\xd1\x80\xd1\x82\xd1\x8b\xd2\x9b \xd0\xb5\xd0\xbb\xd1\x96\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb5 \xd1\x88\xd1\x8b\xd2\x93\xd0\xb0\xd1\x80\xd1\x8b\xd0\xbf \xd1\x82\xd2\xb1\xd1\x80\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb4\xd1\x8b.\n

\xd0\x96\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbb\xd0\xbf\xd1\x8b, \xd0\xb1\xd2\xb1\xd0\xbb \xd0\xb5\xd0\xbb \xd3\x99\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbc\xd0\xbd\xd1\x96\xd2\xa3 80-\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbd \xd0\xb0\xd1\x80\xd1\x82\xd1\x8b\xd2\x9b \xd0\xb5\xd0\xbb\xd0\xbc\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbd \xd0\xb1\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbb\xd1\x81\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb4\xd1\x96 \xd1\x81\xd0\xb0\xd1\x83\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb0-\xd1\x8d\xd0\xba\xd0\xbe\xd0\xbd\xd0\xbe\xd0\xbc\xd0\xb8\xd0\xba\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbb\xd1\x8b\xd2\x9b \xd0\xb1\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb9\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbd\xd1\x8b\xd1\x81\xd1\x82\xd0\xb0\xd1\x80 \xd0\xb6\xd0\xb0\xd1\x81\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb9\xd0\xb4\xd1\x8b.\n

\xd2\x9a\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb7\xd0\xb0\xd2\x9b\xd1\x81\xd1\x82\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbd \xd0\xbc\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbd \xd0\xa2\xd2\xaf\xd1\x80\xd1\x96\xd0\xba\xd0\xbc\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbd\xd1\x81\xd1\x82\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbd \xd0\xb0\xd1\x80\xd0\xb0\xd1\x81\xd1\x8b\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb0\xd2\x93\xd1\x8b \xd2\x9b\xd2\xb1\xd1\x80\xd0\xbb\xd1\x8b\xd2\x9b\xd1\x82\xd0\xb0\xd2\x93\xd1\x8b \xd1\x88\xd0\xb5\xd0\xba\xd0\xb0\xd1\x80\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbd\xd1\x8b\xd2\xa3 \xd2\xb1\xd0\xb7\xd1\x8b\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb4\xd1\x8b\xd2\x93\xd1\x8b 426 \xd0\xba\xd0\xbc. \xd0\x9e\xd0\xbb 2001 \xd0\xb6. \xd1\x88\xd1\x96\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbd\xd1\x96\xd2\xa3 5-\xd1\x96\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb5 \xd1\x80\xd0\xb0\xd1\x82\xd0\xb8\xd1\x84\xd0\xb8\xd0\xba\xd0\xb0\xd1\x86\xd0\xb8\xd1\x8f\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbd\xd2\x93\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbd \xd0\xb5\xd0\xba\xd1\x96\xd0\xb6\xd0\xb0\xd2\x9b\xd1\x82\xd1\x8b \xd0\xba\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbb\xd1\x96\xd1\x81\xd1\x96\xd0\xbc-\xd1\x88\xd0\xb0\xd1\x80\xd1\x82\xd0\xbf\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbd \xd1\x82\xd0\xbe\xd0\xbb\xd1\x8b\xd2\x93\xd1\x8b\xd0\xbc\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbd \xd1\x88\xd0\xb5\xd0\xb3\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb3\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbd.\n
